caAERS CAAERS-4030 New CSM Auth Tag Task Resolved Critical Fixed Ion Olaru Biju Joseph 6/7/2010 20:18 6/9/2010 15:10 Version 2.1.2 Version 2.2-M2
Version 2.2		 Module 13: Security
The caBIG Clinical Trials Suite		 8-Jun-10 0   28800 28800   0%     caAERS v. 2.1.3-SNAPSHOT (2010-05-28 03:36:51) The CSMAccessControlTag has to be modified

Should accept the following parameters
1. domainObject (eg: gov.nih.nci.cabig.caaers.domain.AdverseEvent)
- May be null, if objectPrivilege is provided.

2. hasPrivileges (eg: CREATE)
- The default : "READ"

3. objectPrivilege (eg: gov.nih.nci.cabig.caaers.domain.AdverseEvent:CREATE&UPDATE)
- The objectPrivilege takes precedence, so if provided "domainObject" and "hasPrivileges" are ignored.

Examples of some complex syntaxes
a. <csmauthz:accesscontrol objectPrivilege="gov.nih.nci.cabig.caaers.domain.AdverseEvent#startDate:CREATE|UPDATE" />
b. <csmauthz:accesscontrol objectPrivilege="gov.nih.nci.cabig.caaers.domain.AdverseEvent:CREATE|UPDATE|gov.nih.nci.cabig.caaers.domain.Study:DELETE&ACCESS" />

Should do the following:
1. Must delegate authz call to CaaersSecurityFacade : checkAuthorization(Authentication auth, String objectId, String privilege):boolean;
2. Must cache the authz decision
3. Must use a helper to parse the objectPrivilege syntax
4. Must use a helper class to convert domainObject (java.lang.Object type) to equivalent protection group name. (also for caaers names to be converted to equivalent protection group name) CAAERS-4036 tracks this.
5. Must have proper testcases

caAERS CAAERS-4098 CAAERS-4067
Implement a Filter that will create a purely fabricated Authentication object		 Sub-task Resolved Major Fixed Denis Krylov Biju Joseph 6/24/2010 22:11 7/8/2010 11:36   Version 2.2-M2
Version 2.2		 Module 13: Security
The caBIG Clinical Trials Suite
User Interface		   0   28800 0 37800 131%       Problem Statement :
================
Biju is Person and Organization Admin (PO) at Mayo and User Admin (UA) at Wake

Srini is a research staff at Mayo
Ion is a research staff at Wake

So if Biju search for Research Staff, he will see Srini and Ion. Due to our current architecture/design
1. Biju will be able to provide "login/role" information for Srini,
2. Biju will be able to modify name&contact information of Ion.
which is wrong.

Reason :
======
The UI works based on the Union of roles that Biju has.

Solution :
=======
Need make sure that when Biju is editing Srini, the authentication object has only "PO" granted authority.

How:
=====
We will introduce a Servlet Filter, that will run after the acegi filter, which will do the following.
Pre Process:
1. Find the entity in context,
2. Ask CSM/Security Facade to give the instance level roles that the logged-in person can perform on that entity. (Note :- Biju may not be a research staff in caAERS, based on CSM's instance level authorization we should derive what are the role Biju has on Srini)
3. Populate a fabricated "Authentication" object, consisting of only the required Granted authorities.
4. Store that fabricated "Authentication" as a ThreadLocal variable under the key "CAAERS_FABRICATED_AUTHENTICATION".
5. Store the entity id as a ThreadLocal variable under the key "ENTITY_CACHE_KEY"

Post process:
5. Finally will clear off "CAAERS_FABRICATED_AUTHENTICATION" and ENTITY_CACHE_KEY
   100% 100% 37800 0 28800
